Let's try a different strategy to find the pillow.\\ \tt \\ \tt > go to kitchen\\ \tt Next actions: recheck the kitchen for any hidden spots or areas that haven't been thoroughly examined yet; if the pillow is not found, return to the living room and check again, especially in less obvious places. Once the pillow is found, proceed to the table to complete the goal. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
